20693409_19|20693409|25871|#section_info|0:0|To investigate further the effects of the BR-activated ZmMPK5 on the BR-induced apoplastic H2O2 accumulation, the kinetics of inhibition by the MAPKK inhibitors in the BR-induced apoplastic H2O2 accumulation were examined. 20693409_21|20693409|25871|#section_info|0:0|To investigate further the effects of the BR-activated ZmMPK5 on the BR-induced apoplastic H2O2 accumulation, the kinetics of inhibition by the MAPKK inhibitors in the BR-induced apoplastic H2O2 accumulation were examined.
